       33 +export const getGraph = async (docIds?: string[]): Promise<KGG
          +raph> => {                                                    
       34 +  let ids = docIds                                            
       35 +  if (!ids) {                                                 
       36 +    try {                                                     
       37 +      const docs = await listDocs()

       39 +        .filter(d => d.status === 'ready' || (d as any).status

       41 +    } catch {                                                 
       42 +      ids = []                                                
       43 +    }                                                         
       44 +  }

       47 +    request.get<KGGraph>('/kg/graph', { params: { doc_ids: ids
          +!.join(',') } }),                                             
       48 +    EMPTY_GRAPH                                               
       49 +  )

      48 +def _parse_steps(raw: str):                                    
      49 +    """尽力把 LLM 返回的 JSON 字符串解析成数组；失败返回 None，
         +由前端按 raw 文本继续兼容。"""                                 
      50 +    if not raw:                                                
      51 +        return None                                            
      52 +    s = raw.strip()                                            
      53 +    # 去掉常见的 ```json ... ``` 包裹                          
      54 +    s = re.sub(r"^```(?:json)?\s*", "", s)                     
      55 +    s = re.sub(r"\s*```$", "", s)                              
      56 +    # 截取首个 [ 到末尾的 ]                                    
      57 +    lb = s.find("[")                                           
      58 +    rb = s.rfind("]")                                          
      59 +    if lb >= 0 and rb > lb:                                    
      60 +        s = s[lb : rb + 1]                                     
      61 +    try:                                                       
      62 +        data = json.loads(s)                                   
      63 +        if isinstance(data, list):                             
      64 +            return data                                        
      65 +    except Exception:                                          
      66 +        return None                                            
      67 +    return None                                                
      68 +                                                               
      69 +

      108 +def list_tools(tid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db), _=Depe
          +nds(get_current_user)):                                       
      109 +    t = db.query(Ticket).get(tid)                             
      110 +    if not t: raise HTTPException(404, detail="工单不存在")   
      111 +    out, seen = [], set()                                     
      112 +    steps = t.steps if isinstance(t.steps, list) else []      
      113 +    for st in steps:                                          
      114 +        for name in (st.get("tools") or []):                  
      115 +            key = str(name).strip()                           
      116 +            if key and key not in seen:

      123 +@router.get("/{tid}/manuals")                                 
      124 +def list_manuals(tid: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db), _=De
          +pends(get_current_user)):                                     
      125 +    t = db.query(Ticket).get(tid)                             
      126 +    if not t: raise HTTPException(404, detail="工单不存在")   
      127 +    try:                                                      
      128 +        from app.services.rag import search                   
      129 +        query = f"{t.device} {t.fault}".strip() or t.fault    
      130 +        hits = search(query, k=5)                             
      131 +    except Exception:                                         
      132 +        return []                                             
      133 +    out, seen = [], set()                                     
      134 +    for h in hits:                                            
      135 +        meta = h.get("metadata") or {}                        
      136 +        doc_id = meta.get("doc_id")                           
      137 +        if doc_id is None or doc_id in seen:                  
      138 +            continue                                          
      139 +        seen.add(doc_id)                                      
      140 +        # distance 越小越相似（cosine），换成 0~1 score       
      141 +        dist = h.get("distance")                              
      142 +        score = max(0.0, 1.0 - dist) if isinstance(dist, (int,
          + float)) else 0.0                                             
      143 +        out.append({                                          
      144 +            "docId": str(doc_id),                             
      145 +            "title": meta.get("title") or f"doc-{doc_id}",    
      146 +            "matchedSection": (h.get("content") or "")[:80],  
      147 +            "score": round(score, 3),                         
      148 +        })                                                    
      149 +    return out
